In this case Jitendra Mohan Sharma, Vice President and Senior Advocate of the Supreme Courtbar Association, said that the Supreme Court should reconsider its decision under Article 137 of the Constitution Have got the right to do
 yah adhikaar sirf supreme court ke paas he
 Apart from the Supreme Court, no court or tribunal in India has the right to reconsider its decision
 supreme court ke senior edwocket jitendra mohan sharma ne bataaya ki ayodhya maamle ke pakshakaar punarvichaar yachika daayar kar sakate hai
 He said that the reconsideration petition in the Supreme Court has to be filed within a month of the decision
 ek sawaal ke jawaab main senior edwocket jitendra mohan sharma ne kaha ki supreme court main daakhil hone vaali 99
 9% of the reconsideration petitions are dismissed
 sirf 0
 1 per cent reconsideration petitions are heard
 unhone yah bhi bataaya ki punarvichaar yachika supreme court kii usee bench ke samaksh daakhil kii jaati he, jisane faisla sunaaya he
 When Senior Advocate Jitendra Mohan Sharma has been asked whether Chief Justice Ranjan Gogoi, who is adjudicating on the Ayodhya case, is retiring, will a new bench be set up to reconsider the case, Senior Advocate Sharma said that the Chief The second justice will be included in the bench in place of Justice Ranjan Gogoi
 haalanki baaki bench main shaamil 4 justise vahi rahenge
 Jitendra Mohan Sharma, vice-chairman of the Supreme Court Bar Association, also said that if the reconsideration petition in the Ayodhya case is dismissed, curative petitionation can be filed
 ayodhya maamle main kya tha supreme court kaa faisla?aapako bataa den ki supreme court ke 5 nyaayamurtiyon kii peeth ne ayodhya maamle main 9 november ko ramalala virajman ke paksh main faisla sunaaya tha
 Also, the Sunni Waqf Board had ordered a separate five-acre land in Ayodhya itself
 supreme court ne sunni vakf board ko paanch acre alag se jameen dene kaa faisla anuchhed 142 ke tahat mili adhikaar kaa istemaal karte hue diya tha
 Apart from this, the Supreme Court rejected the claim of Nirmohi Akhara and Shia Waqf Board, the parties to the Ayodhya case
 pehali baar america seenet main raashtrapati donald trump ko bada jhatka laga he
 a resolution against Trump's decision has been passed with a majority
 darasal, america seenet ne syria or afghanistan se sainikon ko waapas bulaane ke raashtrapati donald trump ke faisle ke khilaaf baari bahumat se ek mahatvapurn prastaav paarit kiya he
 Trump's own Republican Party mps also voted in favor of the proposal, which clarified differences within the political party
 seenet main republican netaa mitch mcconell ne prastaav ko sadan ke patal par rakhaa
 He said last week that the proposal would accept the obvious fact that al-qaeda, ISIS and their affiliated organizations in Syria and Afghanistan remain a serious threat to our nation
 prastaav baari bahumat se paarit hua
 70 votes were cast in favor of the motion while 26 votes were opposed
 sadan ke 53 republican seenetteron main se keval teen ne hi iskaa virodh kiya
 Eventually, this amendment will be incorporated into a comprehensive security law on south-west Asia
 prastaav ke anusaar, donon main se kisi bhi desh se sena ko waapas bulaane par ham badi mushkil se haath aayi safalataa gavaan sakate hai or america ke rashtriya suraksha ko bhi khatre main daal sakate hai
 In December, Donald Trump tweeted a plan to withdraw 2,000 US troops from Syria, arguing that the Islamic State group had been conquered
 haalanki, pichley hafte america khufia pramukhon ne soochna di thi ki ye jihadi samooh abhi bhi ek gambhir khatra bane hue hai or apana paanv pasaarne kii firaaq main hai
 Significantly, along with Democrats, many prominent Republican senators have also been critical of Trump's move
 north emsidi ne house tex ke record main property honor kaa naam judwane yaa i-muteshan karwaane ke liye lagane vaale charge ko badha diya he
 So far, the charge levied at Rs 150 has been increased to a maximum of Rs 1500
 is prastaav ko sthai samiti ne bhi paas kar diya he
 According to the corporation till now a nominal amount of 50 rupees was being charged for this process, but in June this year, when the process of mutation was completely made online, it started charging Rs 150
 ab nigam adhikariyon kaa tark he kimmuteshan kii prakriyaake online ho jane ke baad se uske rakrakhaav or online portal ko chalaane par kharch zyada ho rahaa he
 Keeping this in mind, this increase has been made
 prastaav ke mutabik ab sanvibhaajan shulk to puraani dar par hi vasula jayega lekin sampatti maalik kii maut ke baad jab namataran yani muteshan 6 maheene baad karaayaa jaataa he to aavedak ko let charge ke bataur nayi daron se shulk jamaa karana hoga jiske tahat sangyojan shulk 500 rupye or sanvibhaajan shulk 1000 rupye hoga yani kul 1500 rupye kaa shulk dey hoga
 The corporation expects that this will significantly increase revenue
 aapako bataa den kinorth emsidimen puri tarah se i-muteshan pranali ko lagu kiya gaya he
 In which the property owner's name, address, phone number etc
 have to be given
 iske alaava jo kagajaat portal par aplod karne hote hai unamem nae sampatti maalik kaa affidavit, cell dead or iske saath hi us sampatti par chukaaye gaye sabhi house tex kii raseeden shaamil hai
 Decisions that have been taking place since the formation of the Standing Committee, let us tell you that in the North MCD, the election of the Standing Committee has been done at the last but since its formation, major decisions are being taken one after the other
 i-muteshan kii daron main badhotaree ke alaava sthai samiti ne haal hi main bina nakshe main pherbadal kiye sampatti ke andar kiye gaye nirmaan ko niyamit karne ke prastaav ko bhi paas kiya he haalanki logon ko iskaa laabh tabhi mil paaegaa jab centre sarkaar ke shahari vikaas mantralay se prastaav ko hari jhandi milegi
 The southwest monsoon reached Kerala on Tuesday
 isamen haalanki chaar din kii deree hui he, lekin mausam vibhaag kaa kahana he ki isamen pareshaan hone vaali koi baat nahin he
 This monsoon is very important for agriculture
 kerala ke kai hisson main haalanki pichley kai dinon se halki barish ho rahi thi, lekin bhartiya mausam vibhaag (iemdi) ne mangalvaar ko hi isaki ghoshnaa kii
 Kottayam, Alappuzha, Ernakulam and Kasaragoday in Kerala received heavy rainfall
 lekin dakshini jilon, kollam or tiruvanantpuram main mausam shushk hi rahaa
 The monsoon accounts for about 80 percent of the rainfall in the country
 isamen thodi bhi deree se arthvyavastha prabhavit ho sakati he, kyonki desh main jin fasalon se krishi utpaada nikalataa he, unamem se kareeb aadhe kii buaai or ropai june-sitambar ke bich hoti he
 Director General of the India Meteorological Department, LS Rathore said in Delhi that the monsoon is expected to reach other parts of the country fast and ahead of schedule
 karnataka main agle kuch dinon main monsoon aa saktaa he
 The monsoon in Kerala usually falls on June 1
 pichley saal rajya main 29 may ko hi monsoon aa gaya tha
 This time the monsoon has been delayed by four days, but according to the Meteorological Department, there is nothing to worry about it
 iskaa kharif fasalon par koi vipareet asar nahin padegaa
 At the same time, agricultural scientist Devinder Sharma has warned about the amount of rain during the monsoon
 unhone kaha, "monsoon main ek yaa do din kii deree se koi fark nahin padataa
 But the most important thing is the quantity of monsoon in the months of June and July, because during this time the kharif crop is planted
 " unhone kaha ki pichley kuch varsho main monsoon sahi samay par aayaa he, lekin rajasthan, gujarat tathaa bihar main badi maatra main barish nahin hui, jiske kaaran fasalon ko nuksaan hua
 Sharma said, "I am worried about the amount of monsoon, because half of our crop production depends on the southwest monsoon
 " Along with the knocking of monsoon in Kerala, the country's capital Delhi also received rain in many areas on Tuesday
 isaki vajah haalanki monsoon nahin, balki pichley kuch dinon se vaataavaran main vyaapt nami rahi
 The weather became pleasant in Delhi on Tuesday afternoon due to light rain and winds, bringing relief to the people from the scorching heat of the past several days
 mausam vibhaag ke anusaar, "pichley kareeb do dinon se vaataavaran main bahut nami thi, jiske kaaran halki barish hui
 "comments jahaan tak dilli main monsoon kii baat he to yah aam taur par june madhya main aata he, lekin mausam vibhaag ke anusaar, is bare main kuch bhi kahana philhal jaldbaaji hogi ki desh kii rajdhani ko barish kii phuhaaren kab bhigoengi
 Meteorological Director BP Yadav told the media, "we can give a specific date of monsoon at the end of this month only after assessing the monsoon activity in other parts of the country
 " Although many parts of Kerala had been receiving light rain for the past several days, the Indian Meteorological Department (IMD) announced it on Tuesday
 kerala ke kottayam, allapuzha, ernakulam or kasargode main baari varsha hui
 But the weather remained dry in the southern districts, Kollam and Thiruvananthapuram
 desh main hone vaali varsha main monsoon kii bhagidaari kareeb 80 pratishat kii hoti he
 a slight delay in this may affect the economy, as almost half of the crops from which agricultural produce comes in the country are sown and planted between June and September
 bhartiya mausam vibhaag ke mahanideshak ales rathore ne dilli main bataaya ki desh ke anya hisson main bhi teji se or nirdhaarit samay se pehle monsoon aane kii sambhaavna he
 Monsoon is expected in Karnataka in the next few days
 kerala main monsoon aamtaur par ek june ko aa jaataa he
 Last year the monsoon arrived in the state on 29 May
 is baar monsoon chaar din kii deree se aayaa he, lekin mausam vibhaag ke anusaar, isamen chintaa karne vaali koi baat nahin he
 This will not have any adverse effect on Kharif crops
 vahiin, krishi vaigyanik devinder sharma ne monsoon ke dauraan barish kii maatra ko lekar chetaya he
 He said, "delay of one or two days in monsoon does not matter
 lekin sabase mahatvapurn baat june va july ke maheenon main monsoon kii maatra he, kyonki isi dauraan kharif fasal kii ropai hoti he
 "he said that the monsoon has come at the right time in the last few years, but Rajasthan, Gujarat and Bihar did not receive large amounts of rain, causing damage to crops
 sharma ne kaha, "main monsoon kii maatra ko lekar chintit hum, kyonki hamaari aadhi fasal kaa utpaadan dakshin-pashchimi monsoon par nirbhar he
 " kerala main monsoon ke dastak dene ke saath-saath desh kii rajdhani dilli main bhi mangalvaar ko kai ilaakon main barish hui
 The reason, however, was not the monsoon, but the prevailing moisture in the atmosphere for the last few days
 dilli main mangalvaar dopaher halki barish hone or hawaaen chalane se mausam khushgavaar ho gaya, jisase logon ko pichley kai dinon kii bheeshan garmi se raahat mili
 According to the Meteorological Department, "there was a lot of moisture in the atmosphere for the last two days, which caused light rain
